Only managed applications can establish a connection with corporate resources, ensuring your personal privacy is maintained. \r\n\r\nNote: VMware Tunnel works in conjunction with and is managed through configurable system settings within the admin console. VMware Tunnel will not operate without the required VMware infrastructure.
